Vāgbhaṭa Rasaratnasamuccaya with Rasaratnasamuccayabodhinīcomm by śubodhavidyābhūṣaṇa and Nityabodhavidyāratna RasaratnasamuccayaṭīkāVRrs yasyānandabhavena maṅgalakalāsaṃbhāvitena sphuradhāmnā siddharasāmṛtena karuṇāvīkṣāsudhāsindhunā bhaktānāṃ prabhavaprasaṃhṛtijarārāgādirogāḥ kṣaṇācchāntiṃ yānti jagatpradhānabhiṣaje tasmai parasmai namaḥ  VRrs ādimaścandrasenaśca laṅkeśaśca viśāradaḥ kapālī mattamāṇḍavyau bhāskaraḥ śūrasenakaḥ  VRrs ratnakośaśca śambhuśca sāttviko naravāhanaḥ indrado gomukhaścaiva kambalir vyāḍireva ca  VRrs nāgārjunaḥ surānando nāgabodhir yaśodhanaḥ khaṇḍaḥ kāpāliko brahmā govindo lampako hariḥ  VRrs saptaviṃśatisaṃkhyākā rasasiddhipradāyakāḥ rasāṅkuśo bhairavaśca nandī svacchandabhairavaḥ  VRrs manthānabhairavaścaiva kākacaṇḍīśvarastathā vāsudeva ṛṣiḥ śṛṅgaḥ kriyātantrasamuccayī  VRrs rasendratilako yogī bhālukī maithilāhvayaḥ mahādevo narendraśca vāsudevo harīśvaraḥ  VRrs eteṣāṃ kriyate nyeṣāṃ tantrāṇyālokya saṃgrahaḥ rasānāmatha siddhānāṃ cikitsārthopayoginām  VRrs sūnunā siṃhaguptasya rasaratnasamuccayaḥ rasoparasalohāni yantrādikaraṇāni ca  VRrs śuddhyarthamapi lohānāṃ tantrādikaraṇāni ca śuddhiḥ sattvaṃ drutirbhasmakaraṇaṃ ca pravakṣyate  VRrs asti nīhāranilayo mahānuttaradiṅmukhe uttuṅgaśṛṅgasaṃghātalaṅghitābhro mahīdharaḥ  VRrs viśrāmāya viyanmārgavilaṅghanaghanaśramaḥ avatīrṇa iva kṣoṇīṃ śaradambumucāṃ gaṇaḥ  VRrs kucoṣmāṇaṃ nirantaram  VRrs saṃcaran kaṭake yasya nidāghe pi divākaraḥ uddāmahimaruddhoṣmā na śītāṃśorvibhidyate  VRrs guhāgṛheṣu kastūrīmṛganābhisugandhiṣu gāyanti yatra kiṃnaryo gaurīpariṇayotsavam
